<Text>Tom and Chris are the absolute best in the business, period! After conducting very thorough research, I spoke with the owners of a few car audio shops that proved to be serious about their work. After meeting with Tom, I realized I found the best place to purchase high quality products from and have extremely professional installation performed. Tom and Chris exceeded my lofty expectations and the system is simply fantastic!

Tom and Chris truly care about their product, their reputation, their tremendously clean installations, but most importantly they genuinely care about their customers.  There is no substitute for very professional, pleasant and knowledgeable people who are extremely honest about their business. Tom and Chris take the time to clarify every single aspect of the system you want to put together and have installed.

There was never a time either of these gentlemen pressured me to upgrade any components or accessories. Through the numerous emails and in-person visits, Tom and I discussed what system options were available to me with the budget I had to work with. When discussing my system, Tom and Chris offered options but always allowed every single system decision to be made by me.  Both of these men are very patient, believe me.

I had an entirely new sound system installed, along with a brand new Viper alarm and LED exterior and interior lighting. A custom box was built for my system and the outcome of that was a very pleasant surprise. Tom took the time to customize the box‚Äôs beauty cover to my taste and even included a logo and a nickname, all on his own doing! He did not have to take the time to add any of those features but he did so because he felt it helped put the finishing touches on an excellent system that was installed beautifully. Even the sound dampening was installed very cleanly and most importantly, very effectively.

Tom and Chris are very detailed when it comes to ensuring the wiring is very neat, very organized, and aesthetically pleasing. They both took the time to be very detailed with the alarm installation and they both ensured I was completely satisfied with the alarm. Chris even programmed the Viper alarm for me, right down the color of the display on the remote. Both Tom and Chris took the time to walk me through the details of what they were doing and had done, step by step, to allow me to see exactly what was transpiring with my car. They even voluntarily stayed after hours to complete work on my car!

It is very obvious that Tom and Chris take great pride in their work and the results shine through. Lastly, they are very honorable men and that is very important. They both told me directly to my face that if anything arises with the system, contact them, bring the car in and they will take care of it. They are an authorized dealer of excellent products such as JL Audio and Kenwood, among many others. They honor warranties on all products they sell and the installation has an excellent warranty as well.

If you are wanting minor installations or upgrades, or are very serious about your car system, bring your car to Street Sound Plus! They also take care of headlights, taillights, back-up cameras‚Ä¶and many other audio and accessory options. Please, do yourself a favor and stop by Street Sound Plus to appreciate what they do in person.

I will take my car, and any other car I may purchase in the future, to Tom and Chris for any and all work they handle because they have proven themselves. Keep in mind that you get what you pay for ladies and gentlemen. If you do something, have it done correctly and with as good a quality product as possible. I will proudly display the Street Sound Plus stickers on my car and will play my system proudly and loudly to prove and deeply appreciate their work.

Thank you very, very much Tom and Chris. You have made my car even more pleasurable to drive and I like the looks and compliments I receive about the awesome system you gentlemen installed.< /Text><pics>None<//pics></record>

<rate>4</rate><response>None</response><Time>1576016400751< /Time>< text>
I am sad to report that I have had, and am continuing to have, a horrible experience with this clinic. At first, I was very pleased with this Urgent Care. I went in last Friday for symptoms which I believed to be consistent with a UTI. I had been to a number of other Urgent Cares in a variety of locations, and this one was by far the quickest to get you into a medical room and seen by a doctor. I also was pleased with the doctor, who analyzed my urine sample and explained that the presence of white blood cells had indicated a likely bladder infection. I was told that he would start me on a course of antibiotics to treat it as such and send my results out to a lab to confirm the diagnosis. He told me that, if after 2-3 days of taking the medication, symptoms were not getting any better, to call the office and he would be able to switch me to a different prescription. I called the office on the 3rd day after my visit (my 4th day taking the antibiotics as I had started the day of my visit). I asked if my lab results had been received yet and was told that, no, they hadn‚Äôt come in. I relayed to the person on the phone that my symptoms had only gotten worse instead of better and asked if I could get a different prescription, as was directed by the doctor who treated me. I was told that, no, I was unable to get a different prescription until the results came in. Another two days passed as I was patiently awaiting results. At this point, I couldn‚Äôt believe I hadn‚Äôt heard back yet, so I called again to ask if results were in. This time, I was told that my results were never sent to the lab and that I was given the results at my visit. I again explained everything the doctor had said to me and how I was told that I would get affirmed results in 3-5 days. The person on the phone, after reviewing my file, had told me that results were not sent because I had ‚Äúdeclined the results be sent out for further testing,‚Äù which absolutely NEVER occurred. The clinic did offer me the option to come back in to get another urine sample to send to the lab, without an actual office visit to bypass the copay. It is now an entire week later, and I am left in excruciating pain and discomfort with still no results. I have asked on several occasions to speak with the doctor who saw me and to try another prescription until my results are in. The people in the office have told me that the only way to get a new prescription is to come in for another office visit, which is a $75 copay for me. I understand that mix ups happen and people make mistakes, but I find it very unfortunate and unprofessional that this clinic has not done its part to make it right and is okay with allowing me to have what is obviously some kind of serious medical condition, left untreated for 7 days with worsening symptoms. I will never seek care here again.

UPDATE: I received a phone call from the manager who sincerely apologized for my experience and offered me a full refund of my initial copay. I am pleased that my concerns were heard and that there was an attempt to resolve the issue in some way.</text>

<text>This was the second time I came to this urgent care facility and once again I had a really great experience! I'm kind of afraid too many people will find out about this treasure and somehow the center won't be able to keep up the services if too many people come! So I'm going against my selfish desire by writing this review.

I had acute bronchitis twice in two months. When I arrived around lunchtime on a Friday, I was feeling pretty lousy and had a terrible chest cough, running nose and that sick feeling in my body.
?
Within about obliterated five minutes or less,  I was taken to a room where the doctors assistant (I can't recall the gentleman's name) came in and checked me out.  Dr hill was not there at that moment so I met with the assistant and he was very attentive and professional.  He saw I was there again with bronchitis symptoms and ordered a chest xray and prescribed some medication.  I was taken to another room where a really nice xray technician named Gerson was there immediately ready to take my chest xray!

This urgent care is unusual because they have an xray machine at their location!!  Gerson told me my xray results would be evaluated by the doctor and I should get a call with the results on Monday. I expressed I had  great anxiety because I was scared that the results would show something bad (I.e., the  "C" word..). I am not good at waiting for test results when it comes to health matters. I always think "this is it". As I believe Woody Allen once said, we are all one diagnosis away from a death sentence. So needless to say I was quite worried!

About an hour after I left, I received a call from the doctor telling me my chest xray results were normal! I almost had a heart attack when I saw the doctor's  office was calling me so soon!  I had just left an hour earlier! I'm sure Gerson, the nice xray tech saw how nervous I was about waiting until Monday for the test results and had my test reviewed right away! I was so relieved and he saved me from having an anxious  weekend!

I have had only great experiences at this Urgent Care. I will always come here when I have an urgent health issue and can't wait to get an appointment with my primary care doctor. This place has equipment like an xray machine that I've never seen another small neighborhood urgent care have. It's so convenient!

Everyone including the front desk staff were nice and caring. I want to thank everyone that helped me! I highly recommend UrgentMD!</text>< Pictures>

107117291446401236439< /userid>
< name>
Ergin Guney< /name>
< Time>
1511389826406< /Time>
< Rating>
4< /Rating>
< text>
Open only on weekdays, this is a reassuringly old-fashioned lunch joint. The portion sizes are large and the prices are reasonable. You wouldn't expect the quality of the food at a place like this to win awards, and it doesn't, but I've never had anything here to complain about. You can expect a few hot entrees that change daily, along with a fairly extensive permanent menu. The selection outside the hot entrees consist mainly of sandwiches, burgers, and salads, though you can also quickly grab a prepackaged bagel with cream cheese. Actually, the quality of their salads may surprise you, and they carry both prepackaged salads as well as at least a ceasar salad that you can order at the counter. You can polish your meal with a pick from among several options of pastries and donuts. Their fridge is stuffed with an impressively wide selection of bottled drinks and their salty snack and candy bar selection is also wider than what I'd consider average for a place of this scale. There are 10 or so small tables inside and two or three two-person tables just outside the door, but no one would call this place spacious. The flow that consists of ordering at the counter, picking up your food, and paying at the cashier is not exactly streamlined, so this ordering-and-paying process could get a little clogged and confusing when things are really busy at the height of the lunch rush. When the place is more empty, you won't even notice any problem with this though.< /text>

< review>
Always a great choice for taste and value. Compared to Panda Express, the food tastes better, the portions are not stingy and more bang for your buck. The lunch staff get to know their customers making them feel welcome - not familiar with night staff, sorry.  It's fast!!  You can drive in, park, walk into restaurant, order, have order filled, pay and walk out in 3 minutes.  Portions are generous and pricing is excellent.  I usually get the B-combo with golden fried fish,  jalape√±o chicken and chow mein.  The dumpling soup is also a great choice, but it takes a small amount of time.  I've been going here since 2002.  It's consistently good everytime.< /review>

<Text>My dog Jackson had been displaying anxious behaviors since I had returned to work. I contacted Romie Lane Pet Hospital to schedule him an appointment. Their front office staff informed me that I had 3 options. I could schedule him an appointment for Sunday, I could drop him off for the day and they would get to him when they had the chance, or I could bring him in between a certain time frame for a work in.

I chose the work in option, and the conversation ended there. We happily waited over an hour for him to be seen (as expected). I received a call from the vet, which to my surprise wasn't Dr. Ponder. Instead it was Dr. Heart Dominguez. He asked if Jackson stayed in a Kennel because his teeth showed signs similar to those of dogs who chew on their cages. I Informed him that his cage door is never shut, and that he has free range. He stated that his teeth showed otherwise. I let him know that Jackson chews on almost everything, except for his kennel. He responded with "yes all dogs do." I continued to try and brainstorm what Jackson could have been chewing on since I knew it wasn't the kennel. Dr. Dominguez insisted that it was the kennel and moved on. I finally reminded him of the main reason we were there (anxiety concerns). He quickly answered that my dog needed to take obedience classes.... funny because if you know my dog he is one of the most obedient dogs you will ever meet. He takes command well from everyone. I tried to inform the vet of this, but he didn't seem interested. He insisted that I needed to take him to get obedience training. I wasn't sure how that would improve his anxiety and didn't receive those answers from the vet either.
I ended that call extremely confused. Finally, the vet handed me back over to the front office staff where I was informed that my visit would be $135. I kindly asked for an explanation because typically my visits cost about $60. She said that it was an Emergency visit. I told her that I wasn't made aware that it was an emergency visit. She stated that in their office a work in and emergency visit are the same thing. I let her know that I was misinformed because they had never previously referred to a work in as an emergency visit. She put me on a brief hold and then came back to tell me that the knows the receptionist I had spoken to (Brittani Balza) told me that it was an emergency visit and that she made it clear of the $135 fee, which she hadn't. I asked to speak to Dr. Ponder, and that was when I learned that Dr. Ponder had sold his business to the new veterinarian. I calmly expressed my concern to Dr. Dominguez (the owner). He was quick to tell me that he believed his front office staff and that he knows they told me about the emergency fee. I was caught off guard at the fact that this business owner was calling me a liar. At this point I was so upset that I said I would pay the emergency fee and take my business elsewhere. Once I made that statement he got extremely agitated and said "don't cut me off, if you would listen then you would know that I am giving you what you want. They will only be charging you $60 for the visit." At this point I am absolutely appalled at the lack of customer service and the way I am being talked to. I told him that that I was not comfortable or happy with him and his staff and that I would still be taking my business elsewhere. He said okay and hung up on me. I called back and was hung up on two more times before being able to pay.
I have never been so disappointed in a business. Not only did my dog receive sub par care, but the treatment I received was disgraceful.
